<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DuPont Delivers Strong EPS Growth on 32% Higher Sales for Third Quarter 2011</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Full-year Earnings Outlook Narrowed to Upper Half of Previous Range</font></i></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Highlights:</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Third quarter 2011 earnings were $.69 per share excluding significant items (see Schedule B) versus $.40 per share in the prior year.&#160; Reported third quarter 2011 earnings were $.48 per share versus $.40 per share in the prior year.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sales increased 32 percent to $9.2 billion with 15 percent higher local prices, 4 percent currency benefit, 1 percent higher volume, and a 12 percent net increase from portfolio changes.&#160; Sales in developing markets grew 38 percent.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Growth in demand for the company&#146;s agricultural products and further expansion into food ingredient and enzyme markets offset destocking in photovoltaics and specialty polymers.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Segment pre-tax operating income excluding significant items increased 50 percent to $1.1 billion, largely driven by improvements in the Performance Chemicals and Agriculture segments and the acquisition of Danisco.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DuPont is on track to meet its full-year 2011 productivity targets for fixed costs and working capital.&#160; Year-to-date fixed cost productivity totals more than $250 million.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Given the strong performance in the third quarter, the company has raised its expectations for full-year 2011 earnings to a range of $3.97 to $4.05 per share excluding significant items.&#160; This moves the range to the upper half of the company&#146;s previous guidance of $3.90 to $4.05 per share.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The resilience and diversity of DuPont&#146;s business portfolio was evident in our strong third quarter results.&#160; Despite turbulent global economic and market conditions, we delivered solid growth through innovative products and process technologies, disciplined execution and continued productivity gains,&#148; said DuPont Chair and CEO Ellen Kullman.&#160; &#147;Our portfolio is further strengthened by the rapid integration of Danisco, continued capacity expansions and selective growth investments across many of our businesses.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">E. I. du Pont de Nemours and Company</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Global Consolidated Sales and Net Income</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2011 consolidated net sales of $9.2 billion were 32 percent higher than the prior year reflecting 15 percent higher local prices, 4 percent favorable currency effect, 1 percent higher volume and a 12 percent net increase from portfolio changes.&#160; The table below shows regional sales and variances versus the third quarter 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">* Europe, Middle East&nbsp;&amp; Africa</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2011 net income attributable to DuPont was $452 million versus $367 million in the third quarter 2010. Excluding significant items, net income attributable to DuPont increased $288 million, or 78 percent, to $655 million.&#160; The increase principally reflects higher selling prices and currency benefit, partly offset by increased spending for selling, marketing and research and development, and increased costs for raw materials, energy, and freight.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2<a name="PB_2_085316_5796"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Earnings Per Share</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The table below shows year-over-year earnings per share (EPS) variances for the third quarter.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="66%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:.5in;width:66.68%;">
<tr>
<td width="100%" colspan="5" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in 0in 0in 0in 0in;width:100.0%;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_090901_7748"></a></font></p>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\105589\11-28507-1\task4919996\28507-1-mm-03.htm',USER='105589',CD='Oct 25 09:38 2011' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following is a summary of business results for each of the company&#146;s reportable segments, comparing third quarter 2011 with third quarter 2010, for sales and PTOI (loss) excluding significant items. References to selling price are on a U.S. dollar basis, including the impact of currency.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Agriculture&nbsp;- </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales of $1.4 billion were up $0.4 billion, or 41 percent, from 26 percent higher volume and 15 percent higher selling prices principally reflecting a strong, early start to the Latin American season.&#160; For Pioneer seed, volume and price growth was delivered in both corn and soybeans.&#160; Crop Protection sales increased across all regions and market segments, led by continued strong demand for Rynaxypyr&#174; insecticide.&nbsp; PTOI of $(69) million improved from $(191) million due to higher sales, partially offset by growth investments and portfolio changes.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Electronics&nbsp;&amp; Communications - </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales of $841 million were up 20 percent, with 28 percent higher selling prices, primarily metals pass-through, and 8 percent lower volume.&#160; Lower volume reflects destocking in photovoltaics, and softness in plasma displays and packaging graphics.&#160; PTOI of $99 million decreased $27 million on lower volume.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Industrial Biosciences - </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales of $293 million and PTOI of $34 million reflect the acquisition of Danisco&#146;s enzyme business.&#160; PTOI includes approximately $4 million of amortization expense associated with the fair value step-up of intangible assets acquired as part of the acquisition.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Nutrition&nbsp;&amp; Health - </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales of $844 million were up $540 million principally due to the acquisition of Danisco&#146;s specialty food ingredients business.&#160; PTOI of $55 million increased $45 million reflecting the acquisition and includes $22 million of amortization expense associated with the fair value step-up of the acquired intangible assets.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Performance Chemicals - </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales of $2.1 billion were up 28 percent, with 29 percent higher selling prices and 1 percent lower volume.&#160; Higher selling prices were driven by strong global demand for titanium dioxide and fluoropolymers and pass-through pricing of higher raw material costs for industrial chemicals.&#160; Volume declined in refrigerants and industrial chemicals.&#160; PTOI of $593 million increased $301 million due to higher selling prices.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Performance Coatings - </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales of $1.1 billion were up 17 percent, with 13 percent higher selling prices and 4 percent higher volume.&#160; Higher selling prices reflect favorable currency and pricing actions across all market segments to offset higher raw material costs.&#160; Demand increased for OEM motor vehicle coatings and remained strong for industrial coatings, particularly in the North American heavy-duty truck market.&#160; PTOI of $72 million increased $8 million on strong sales performance led by refinish.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Performance Materials - </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales of $1.7 billion were up 11 percent, with 18 percent higher selling prices and 7 percent lower volume.&#160; Higher selling prices offset higher raw material costs.&#160; Lower volume reflects broad-based channel destocking along with softening in consumer and industrial markets, and production-related supply issues in ethylene-based polymers.&#160; PTOI of $231 million decreased $50 million on lower volume.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Safety&nbsp;&amp; Protection -</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> Sales of $1.0 billion were up 15 percent, with 8 percent higher selling prices and a 7 percent increase from the MECS acquisition.&#160; Higher selling prices primarily reflect pricing actions to offset raw material cost increases.&#160; PTOI of $118 million decreased $16 million on destocking in industrial markets and higher spending for growth initiatives including the Cooper River Kevlar&#174; expansion, which more than offset the impact of the acquisition and favorable currency.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Additional information is available on the DuPont Investor Center website at www.dupont.com.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_090940_141"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\JMS\105589\11-28507-1\task4919996\28507-1-mm-03.htm',USER='105589',CD='Oct 25 09:38 2011' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Outlook</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Given the strong performance in the third quarter, the company has raised its expectations for<b>  </b>full-year 2011 earnings to a range of $3.97 to $4.05 per share excluding significant items.&#160; This moves the range to the upper half of the company&#146;s previous guidance of $3.90 to $4.05 per share.&#160; Expectations for the fourth quarter include slowing global growth, some destocking, and the recognition that a portion of Agriculture sales in Latin America was shifted to the third quarter by the early start of the planting season.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Use of Non-GAAP Measures</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management believes that certain non-GAAP measurements are meaningful to investors because they provide insight with respect to ongoing operating results of the company.&#160; Such measurements are not recognized in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) and should not be viewed as an alternative to GAAP measures of performance.&#160; Reconciliations of non-GAAP measures to GAAP are provided in schedules C and D.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">DuPont (NYSE: DD) has been bringing world-class science and engineering to the global marketplace in the form of innovative products, materials, and services since 1802.&#160; The company believes that by collaborating with customers, governments, NGOs, and thought leaders we can help find solutions to such global challenges as providing enough healthy food for people everywhere, decreasing dependence on fossil fuels, and protecting life and the environment.&#160; For additional information about DuPont and its commitment to inclusive innovation, please visit http://www.dupont.com.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:&#160; This news release contains forward-looking statements which may be identified by their use of words like &#147;plans,&#148; &#147;expects,&#148; &#147;will,&#148; &#147;believes,&#148; &#147;intends,&#148; &#147;estimates&#148; or other words of similar meaning.&#160; All statements that address expectations or projections about the future, including statements about the company&#146;s growth strategy, product development, regulatory approval, market position, anticipated benefits of acquisitions, outcome of contingencies, such as litigation and environmental matters, expenditures and financial results, are forward-looking statements.&#160; Forward-looking statements are not guarantees of future performance and are based on certain assumptions and expectations of future events which may not be realized.&#160; Forward-looking statements also involve risks and uncertainties, many of which are beyond the company&#146;s control.&#160; Some of the important factors that could cause the company&#146;s actual results to differ materially from those projected in any such forward-looking statements are: fluctuations in energy and raw material prices; failure to develop and market new products and optimally manage product life cycles; significant litigation and environmental matters; failure to appropriately manage process safety and product stewardship issues; changes in laws and regulations or political conditions; global economic and capital markets conditions, such as inflation, interest and currency exchange rates; business or supply disruptions; security threats, such as acts of sabotage, terrorism or war, weather events and natural disasters; inability to protect and enforce the company&#146;s intellectual property rights; and integration of acquired businesses and completion of divestitures of underperforming or non-strategic assets or businesses.&#160; The company undertakes no duty to update any forward-looking statements as a result of future developments or new information.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SCHEDULE B</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<tr>
<td width="33%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:33.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second   quarter and year-to-date 2011 included charges related to the Danisco   acquisition of $(103) recorded in Cost of goods sold and other operating   charges. These charges included $(60) of transaction costs and a $(43) charge   related to the fair value step-up of inventories that were acquired from   Danisco and sold in the second quarter 2011. Pre-tax charges by segment were:   Industrial Biosciences - $(17), Nutrition&nbsp;&amp; Health - $(33), and   Corporate expenses - $(53).</font></p>    </td>   </tr>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third   quarter and year-to-date 2011 included charges related to the Danisco   acquisition of $(171). These charges included $(135) recorded in Cost of   goods sold and other operating charges for $(3)&nbsp;of transaction costs and   a $(132) charge related to the fair value step-up of inventories that were   acquired from Danisco and sold in the third quarter 2011. These charges also   included a $(36) restructuring charge recorded in Employee separation / asset   related charges, net related to severance and related benefit costs. Pre-tax   charges by segment were: Industrial Biosciences - $(61), Nutrition&nbsp;&amp;   Health - $(89), Other - $(18), and Corporate expenses - $(3).</font></p>    </td>   </tr>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third   quarter and year-to-date 2011 included a $(75) charge recorded in Cost of   goods sold and other operating charges associated with the company&#146;s process   to fairly resolve claims associated with the use of Imprelis&#174; herbicide. The   company will continue to evaluate reported claim damage as additional   information becomes available, which could result in future charges that   cannot be reasonably estimated at this time; the company intends to seek   recovery from its insurance carriers for costs associated with this matter in   excess of $100. This matter relates to the Agriculture segment.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">E. I. du Pont de Nemours and Company</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Measures</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(Dollars in millions, except per share amounts)</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SCHEDULE D (continued)</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exchange Gains/Losses</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company routinely uses forward exchange contracts to offset its net exposures, by currency, related to the foreign currency denominated monetary assets and liabilities of its operations. The objective of this program is to maintain an approximately balanced position in foreign currencies in order to minimize, on an after-tax basis, the effects of exchange rate changes.&#160; The net pre-tax exchange gains and losses are recorded in Other income, net on the Consolidated Income Statements and are largely offset by the associated tax impact.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As shown above, the &#147;Total Exchange Gain (Loss)&#148; is the sum of the &#147;Subsidiary/Affiliate Monetary Position Gain (Loss)&#148; and the &#147;Hedging Program Gain (Loss).&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Reconciliation of Base Income Tax Rate to Effective Income Tax Rate</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Base income tax rate is defined as the effective income tax rate less the effect of exchange gains/losses, as defined above, and significant items.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
